## 1. [On a Paving Stone Mounted (1978)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/on-a-paving-stone-mounted-1978?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=on-a-paving-stone-mounted-1978&utm_term=on-a-paving-stone-mounted-1978)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/on-a-paving-stone-mounted-1978?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=on-a-paving-stone-mounted-1978&amp;utm_term=on-a-paving-stone-mounted-1978"><img alt="on-a-paving-stone-mounted-tt0078028-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/on-a-paving-stone-mounted-tt0078028-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"On a Paving Stone Mounted" is a unique and critically acclaimed film from 1978. Directed and written by Thaddeus O'Sullivan, the movie is set in London, England, and is an experimental docudrama that blends real-life stories with creative dramatization. The film revolves around the lives of Irish immigrants and the challenges they face in a new environment. The story portrays their hopes, dreams, and struggles, as well as their integration into the society. The movie is both dramatic and thought-provoking, showcasing the complexities and contradictions of the human experience. Starring Annie Balfour, Paul Bennett, and Gabriel Byrne, the film takes viewers on an emotional journey through the lives of these characters. The exceptional cinematography and sound design further enhance the overall experience. Released by the British Film Institute (BFI), "On a Paving Stone Mounted" is a compelling drama that explores themes of immigration, identity, and community. Despite its vintage release, the movie's message remains relevant and resonates with contemporary audiences. "On a Paving Stone Mounted" has garnered praise and recognition for its innovative approach to storytelling, and has received an impressive IMDb rating of 7.6. With its intriguing plot and strong performances, this film is sure to leave a lasting impression on viewers. 



<br>

- Genres: Drama
- Runtime: 1h 36min
- Directed by: Thaddeus O'Sullivan
- Starring: Annie Balfour, Paul Bennett, Gabriel Byrne
- Box Office:
- IMDb Rating: 7.6

## 2. [Wings of Ash: A Dramatization of the Life of Antonin Artaud (1978)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/wings-of-ash-a-dramatization-of-the-life-of-antonin-artaud-1978?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=wings-of-ash-a-dramatization-of-the-life-of-antonin-artaud-1978&utm_term=wings-of-ash-a-dramatization-of-the-life-of-antonin-artaud-1978)

<br>

Experience the intense and emotional journey of Antonin Artaud in the dramatic short film, "Wings of Ash: A Dramatization of the Life of Antonin Artaud" (1978). This intriguing 10-minute production, directed by Marcus Reichert, delves into the world of the famous French actor and theater director, leaving no stone unturned. The film opens with Dr. Allende, played by Dennis Lipscomb, suggesting that Artaud, portrayed by Mick Jagger, undergoes a psychoanalysis session during his stay at Dr. Allende's home. However, Artaud's response to the proposition is far from pleasant, leading to an emotionally charged interaction that shines a light on his inner struggles. "Wings of Ash" showcases the incredible performances of its star-studded cast and explores the depths of Artaud's complex character. This short, yet captivating piece offers a unique glimpse into the life of a groundbreaking artist, making it a must-watch for fans of drama and biographies alike. With an IMDb rating of 6.0 and IMDb rating votes of 9.0, "Wings of Ash" has left an impact on audiences and continues to garner interest today. Embrace the world of Antonin Artaud and immerse yourself in this thought-provoking and intriguing short film.

## 3. [The Outsider (1979)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-outsider-1979?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=the-outsider-1979&utm_term=the-outsider-1979)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-outsider-1979?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=the-outsider-1979&amp;utm_term=the-outsider-1979"><img alt="the-outsider-tt0079687-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/the-outsider-tt0079687-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

Prepare to be taken on a thrilling and suspenseful journey through the dark underbelly of political intrigue with The Outsider (1979). This intense drama transports audiences to 1970s Ireland, where a young American man, lured by the allure of the IRA, finds himself entangled in a web of deception and manipulation. Touting an impressive cast, including Craig Wasson, Sterling Hayden, and Patricia Quinn, The Outsider delves into the world of political propaganda and covert operations. As the protagonist struggles to reconcile his ideals with his newfound role in the IRA, he realizes that he has been duped into participating in a dangerous and ruthless scheme. Directed by Tony Luraschi and written by Colin Leinster and Tony Luraschi, The Outsider masterfully combines elements of drama, history, and thriller genres to create an unforgettable cinematic experience. With a runtime of 2 hours and 2 minutes, the film provides ample time to explore the complexity of its central themes, leaving audiences on the edge of their seats until the last frame. The Outsider received an IMDb rating of 6.8 based on 316.0 votes, with a significant box office success, grossing an estimated $3 million. If you're looking for a movie that will keep you guessing and prove that the truth can be more dangerous than the pursuit, look no further than The Outsider.

## 4. [Excalibur (1981)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/excalibur-1981?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=excalibur-1981&utm_term=excalibur-1981)

"Excalibur" (1981) is a captivating blend of adventure, drama, and fantasy that delves into the legendary tale of Arthur Pendragon and his ascent to unite the Britons under the banner of the Round Table of Camelot. Directed by John Boorman and featuring an all-star cast including Nigel Terry, Helen Mirren, and Nicholas Clay, "Excalibur" has garnered numerous accolades, including an Oscar nomination and a 7.3 IMDb rating. Set against the backdrop of a mystical world, "Excalibur" follows the journey of Arthur as he rises to power with the guidance of the wise and powerful Merlin. Together, they forge a realm of justice and prosperity, but dark forces threaten to unravel their vision. As Arthur navigates the complexities of love, loyalty, and betrayal, he must rely on the mythical Excalibur to safeguard his kingdom and fulfill his destiny. With its rich production design and stunning visual effects, "Excalibur" immerses viewers in the enchanting world of Arthurian legend, bringing to life the timeless tale of valor, honor, and the quest for the Holy Grail. Embark on this unforgettable journey, and witness the unraveling of destiny and the power of camaraderie in the face of adversity.

In the tense and dramatic film Hanna K. , an Israeli lawyer takes on a complex case defending a Palestinian charged by the Israeli-Occupied Territories' Military Court System. The strong political background of the case complicates the situation, as both sides fight for justice amidst escalating tensions. Directed by the renowned Costa-Gavras, this powerful drama stars Jill Clayburgh, Jean Yanne, and Gabriel Byrne, with the narrative unfolding in two distinct countries. Hanna K. is a thought-provoking, independent film that explores the complex nature of conflicts and the relentless pursuit of truth.

## 6. [The Rocking Horse Winner (1983)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-rocking-horse-winner-1983?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=the-rocking-horse-winner-1983&utm_term=the-rocking-horse-winner-1983)

<br>

The Rocking Horse Winner, a critically acclaimed independent film from 1983, is a haunting short drama inspired by the classic novella by D. H. Lawrence. The story follows the life of Paul, a young boy from a family constantly in search of financial security. As the tension in his household mounts, Paul becomes obsessed with finding luck to provide for his family, even at the cost of his own well-being. The film's haunting visuals and powerful performances by Eleanor David, Charles Keating, and Charles Hathorn make it a compelling experience for fans of drama and short films. Directed by Robert Bierman with a screenplay by Howard Schuman, The Rocking Horse Winner has earned an impressive 8.0 IMDb rating and two BAFTA Award nominations. This eerie, poignant tale is one not to be missed. 



<br>

- Genres: Drama, Short, Fantasy
- Runtime: 33min

"Reflections, " a poignant romance-drama film set in the idyllic Irish countryside, explores the unexpected bonds formed between a stoic historian and the dysfunctional Lawless family. Our protagonist, a man known for his scholarly pursuits, settles into a lodge to complete his biography of Sir Isaac Newton. However, his attention shifts to the entangled relationships within the Lawless family, including an aunt and niece. Unraveling layers of emotion, the historian finds himself drawn into the family's personal lives, grappling with the complexities of love and attachment. "Reflections" expertly weaves a tale of love and human connection, providing a captivating cinematic experience.

## 9. [Defense of the Realm (1985)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/defense-of-the-realm-1985?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=defense-of-the-realm-1985&utm_term=defense-of-the-realm-1985)

In 1985, the political thriller "Defense of the Realm" unfolds a suspenseful narrative, where a tenacious newspaper reporter uncovers a potential spy amongst the ranks of a Member of Parliament. As the story unfolds, the reporter is thrust into an intricate web of political dramas and uncovers a massive cover-up that goes far beyond his initial suspicions. Directed by David Drury and written by Martin Stellman, the film stars Gabriel Byrne, Greta Scacchi, and Denholm Elliott. Produced by The Rank Organisation, National Film Finance Corporation (NFFC), and Enigma Productions, "Defense of the Realm" delivers a thrilling experience set in the United Kingdom with an English language runtime of 1 hour and 36 minutes. This 1986 release, with a content rating of PG, garnered one BAFTA award, 7 wins, and 2 nominations in total. With a runtime of 1 hour and 36 minutes, "Defense of the Realm" offers an engaging and suspenseful experience for viewers interested in political intrigue, journalism, and undercover espionage. The film's IMDb rating of 6.5, based on 2,471 votes, indicates a compelling and suspenseful movie-going experience.

## 72. [The Bridge of San Luis Rey (2004)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-bridge-of-san-luis-rey-2004?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=the-bridge-of-san-luis-rey-2004&utm_term=the-bridge-of-san-luis-rey-2004)

"The Bridge of San Luis Rey" (2004) is a dramatic, historical, and romantic film set in 18th century Peru. Directed by Mary McGuckian and written by both McGuckian and Thornton Wilder, the film follows a friar who finds himself in the crosshairs of the Inquisition after questioning God's intentions in the collapse of an Andean rope bridge, resulting in the deaths of five individuals. Michael Des Barres: Who Do You Want Me to Be? is a riveting documentary that explores the extraordinary life and career of Michael Des Barres, an enigmatic figure and master of reinvention. Born to a junkie aristocrat and a schizophrenic showgirl, Michael's journey through the world of rock and roll, television, and movies spans over 50 years, making him a true legend in the entertainment industry. J. Elvis Weinstein, the director, takes us on a captivating ride as he delves into Michael's personal life and professional achievements, shedding light on his constant quest for self-discovery and transformation. Featuring interviews with notable figures in the entertainment industry, such as Allison Anders and Ed Begley Jr. , as well as Robbie Blunt, Michael's bandmate in Black Bone Chicken, this film offers a never-before-seen perspective on the life and career of a true icon who has managed to captivate audiences across generations. With a runtime of 1h 22min, Michael Des Barres: Who Do You Want Me to Be? is a must-watch for any fan of the rock and roll era, as it provides an intimate look into the life of a remarkable individual who has left an indelible mark on the entertainment world.

## 108. "My Astonishing Self: Gabriel Byrne on George Bernard Shaw" (2017) is an intriguing documentary that delves into the fascinating life and works of Irish playwright George Bernard Shaw. Narrated by renowned actor Gabriel Byrne, this compelling film offers a fresh perspective on the Nobel laureate's extraordinary career and personal beliefs. Byrne shares captivating insights and anecdotes that shed light on Shaw's extraordinary journey as an influential figure in literature and public life.
